uniform 
uniform sampler2D y_tex;
uniform sampler2D u_tex;
uniform sampler2D v_tex;
vec4 sample(vec2 p) {
  float y = texture2D(y_tex, p).r * 1.16438;
  float u = texture2D(u_tex, p).r;
  float v = texture2D(v_tex, p).r;
  return vec4(y + 1.59603 * v - 0.874202,
    y - 0.391762 * u - 0.812968 * v + 0.531668,
    y + 2.01723 * u - 1.08563, 1);
}

uniform vec2 xUnit;
uniform vec4 coeffs;

void main() {
  gl_FragColor.r = coeffs.a + dot(coeffs.rgb,
      sample(tc - 1.5 * xUnit).rgb);
  gl_FragColor.g = coeffs.a + dot(coeffs.rgb,
      sample(tc - 0.5 * xUnit).rgb);
  gl_FragColor.b = coeffs.a + dot(coeffs.rgb,
      sample(tc + 0.5 * xUnit).rgb);
  gl_FragColor.a = coeffs.a + dot(coeffs.rgb,
      sample(tc + 1.5 * xUnit).rgb);
}
